                        0

                    `plan_time`,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    1,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_task`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        `spen_time`, 
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_time`,

                    `status_calender`='accepted',

                        1,
                        0

            ) AS `actual_task`,

                        1,
                        0
                    )
                )

2024-11-05 16:19:10
- Server 		: Prod
- User 			: arieftyarto@mastersystem.co.id
- Module 		: productivity
- SubModule		: chart_productivity
- Status 		: No database selected
- Query 		: SELECT 
        resource_email, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_imp, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_imp, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_mnt, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_mnt, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_non, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_non, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_si,
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_si,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)))) AS task_imp_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)))) AS time_imp_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)))) AS task_mnt_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)))) AS time_mnt_progress,
		(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))) AS total

    FROM sa_trx_productivity 
    WHERE

- Query 		: SELECT 
		resource_email,
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) AS accepted, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) AS declined, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) AS needsAction, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0)) AS tentative, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = NULL, 1, 0)) AS `null`,
		(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender IS NULL, 1, 0))) AS total_task,
		(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)))/(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender IS NULL, 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0))) AS progress
	FROM sa_trx_productivity 
	WHERE
		tracked_date >= '2024-10-18' AND 
		tracked_date <= '2024-11-01'
		 AND `resource_email` IN ('Cornelius Aji Nugroho<cornelius.aji@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Mulyadi Indra<mulyadi.indra@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Ahmad Solahudin Rifandi<ahmad.solahudin@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Fatih Khoiri<fatih.khoiri@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Chandra Halim Nuruddin<chandra.halim@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Bambang Ary Nugroho<bambang.ary@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Tegar Virgiawan<tegar.virgiawan@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Teguh M Wahyu Akbar<teguh.wahyu@mastersystem.co.id>', 'I Dewa Putu Suyoga Nalaswara<suyoga.nalaswara@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Setyo Pambudi<setyo.pambudi@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Rahmat Arizal Putra<rahmat.arizal@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Fabian Darryl Enrico<fabian.darryl@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Muhammad Ikhsan Hidayatullah<ikhsan.hidayatullah@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Achmad Rifki Ansyori<achmad.rifki@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Muhammad Fadhil<fadhil.muhammad@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Khalid Hamzah Haza Al Hamami<khalid.hamzah@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Rahmadani Sudarno<rahmadani.sudarno@mastersystem.co.id>')

- SubModule		: dashboard_productivity
- Status 		: No database selected
- Query 		: SELECT `resource_email`, 
            `project_type`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    `plan_time`,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    1,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_task`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        `spen_time`, 
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        1,
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_task`,
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `project_type`='MSI Project Implementation',
                    1,
                    IF(
                        `project_type`='MSI Project Maintenance',
                        1,
                        0
                    )
                )
            ) AS `total_project` 
        FROM `sa_trx_productivity` 
        WHERE 
            `task_date` >= '2024-10-29' 
            AND `task_date` <= '2024-11-12' 
             
             
            AND `resource_email` IN ('Arieftyarto Taufiq Ramadhan<arieftyarto@mastersystem.co.id>')
            AND ((DAYOFWEEK(`task_date`) BETWEEN 2 AND 6) OR `work_on_weekends`=1)
        GROUP BY `project_type`

- Query 		: SELECT 
        resource_email, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_imp, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_imp, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_mnt, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_mnt, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_non, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_non, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_si,
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_si,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)))) AS task_imp_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)))) AS time_imp_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)))) AS task_mnt_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)))) AS time_mnt_progress,
		(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))) AS total

    FROM sa_trx_productivity 
    WHERE

- Query 		: SELECT 
		resource_email,
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) AS accepted, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) AS declined, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) AS needsAction, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0)) AS tentative, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = NULL, 1, 0)) AS `null`,
		(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender IS NULL, 1, 0))) AS total_task,
		(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)))/(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender IS NULL, 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0))) AS progress
	FROM sa_trx_productivity 
	WHERE
		tracked_date >= '2024-10-30' AND 
		tracked_date <= '2024-11-05'
		 AND `resource_email` IN ('Cornelius Aji Nugroho<cornelius.aji@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Mulyadi Indra<mulyadi.indra@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Ahmad Solahudin Rifandi<ahmad.solahudin@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Fatih Khoiri<fatih.khoiri@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Chandra Halim Nuruddin<chandra.halim@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Bambang Ary Nugroho<bambang.ary@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Tegar Virgiawan<tegar.virgiawan@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Teguh M Wahyu Akbar<teguh.wahyu@mastersystem.co.id>', 'I Dewa Putu Suyoga Nalaswara<suyoga.nalaswara@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Setyo Pambudi<setyo.pambudi@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Rahmat Arizal Putra<rahmat.arizal@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Fabian Darryl Enrico<fabian.darryl@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Muhammad Ikhsan Hidayatullah<ikhsan.hidayatullah@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Achmad Rifki Ansyori<achmad.rifki@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Muhammad Fadhil<fadhil.muhammad@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Khalid Hamzah Haza Al Hamami<khalid.hamzah@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Rahmadani Sudarno<rahmadani.sudarno@mastersystem.co.id>')

2024-11-05 19:18:44
- Server 		: Prod
- User 			: iwan@mastersystem.co.id
- Module 		: productivity
- SubModule		: dashboard_productivity
- Status 		: No database selected
- Query 		: SELECT `resource_email`, 
            `project_type`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    `plan_time`,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    1,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_task`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        `spen_time`, 
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        1,
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_task`,
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `project_type`='MSI Project Implementation',
                    1,
                    IF(
                        `project_type`='MSI Project Maintenance',
                        1,
                        0
                    )
                )
            ) AS `total_project` 
        FROM `sa_trx_productivity` 
        WHERE 
            `task_date` >= '2024-10-29' 
            AND `task_date` <= '2024-11-12' 
             
             
            AND `resource_email` IN ('Iwan<iwan@mastersystem.co.id>')
            AND ((DAYOFWEEK(`task_date`) BETWEEN 2 AND 6) OR `work_on_weekends`=1)
        GROUP BY `project_type`

- Server 		: Prod
- User 			: iwan@mastersystem.co.id
- Module 		: productivity
- SubModule		: chart_productivity
- Status 		: No database selected
- Query 		: SELECT 
        resource_email, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_imp, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_imp, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_mnt, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_mnt, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_non, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_non, 
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) AS total_time_si,
        SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)) AS total_task_si,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)))) AS task_imp_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)))) AS time_imp_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0), 0)))) AS task_mnt_progress,
        (SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))/(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))+SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)))) AS time_mnt_progress,
		(SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Implementation", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Project Maintenance", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Non-Project", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0)) + SUM(IF(project_type = "MSI Self Improvement", IF(status_calender = "accepted", spen_time, 0), 0))) AS total

    FROM sa_trx_productivity 
    WHERE

- Server 		: Prod
- User 			: iwan@mastersystem.co.id
- Module 		: productivity
- SubModule		: chart_productivity
- Status 		: No database selected
- Query 		: SELECT 
		resource_email,
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) AS accepted, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) AS declined, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) AS needsAction, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0)) AS tentative, 
		SUM(IF(status_calender = NULL, 1, 0)) AS `null`,
		(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender IS NULL, 1, 0))) AS total_task,
		(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)))/(SUM(IF(status_calender = "accepted", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "declined", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "needsAction", 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender IS NULL, 1, 0)) + SUM(IF(status_calender = "tentative", 1, 0))) AS progress
	FROM sa_trx_productivity 
	WHERE
		tracked_date >= '2024-10-30' AND 
		tracked_date <= '2024-11-05'
		 AND `resource_email` IN ('Cornelius Aji Nugroho<cornelius.aji@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Mulyadi Indra<mulyadi.indra@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Ahmad Solahudin Rifandi<ahmad.solahudin@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Fatih Khoiri<fatih.khoiri@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Chandra Halim Nuruddin<chandra.halim@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Bambang Ary Nugroho<bambang.ary@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Tegar Virgiawan<tegar.virgiawan@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Teguh M Wahyu Akbar<teguh.wahyu@mastersystem.co.id>', 'I Dewa Putu Suyoga Nalaswara<suyoga.nalaswara@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Setyo Pambudi<setyo.pambudi@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Rahmat Arizal Putra<rahmat.arizal@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Fabian Darryl Enrico<fabian.darryl@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Muhammad Ikhsan Hidayatullah<ikhsan.hidayatullah@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Achmad Rifki Ansyori<achmad.rifki@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Muhammad Fadhil<fadhil.muhammad@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Khalid Hamzah Haza Al Hamami<khalid.hamzah@mastersystem.co.id>', 'Rahmadani Sudarno<rahmadani.sudarno@mastersystem.co.id>')

- Query 		: SELECT `resource_email`, 
            `project_type`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    `plan_time`,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    1,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_task`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        `spen_time`, 
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        1,
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_task`,
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `project_type`='MSI Project Implementation',
                    1,
                    IF(
                        `project_type`='MSI Project Maintenance',
                        1,
                        0
                    )
                )
            ) AS `total_project` 
        FROM `sa_trx_productivity` 
        WHERE 
            `task_date` >= '2024-10-29' 
            AND `task_date` <= '2024-11-12' 
             
             
            AND `resource_email` IN ('Tegar Virgiawan<tegar.virgiawan@mastersystem.co.id>')
            AND ((DAYOFWEEK(`task_date`) BETWEEN 2 AND 6) OR `work_on_weekends`=1)
        GROUP BY `project_type`
